This feature validates that a CSV/text file's header row column names match the target table's column names (in order and spelling).\n\n## 1. Feature Syntax\n```sql\nCOPY table_name FROM 'file' WITH (HEADER MATCH, FORMAT CSV);\nCOPY table_name FROM 'file' WITH (HEADER MATCH);  -- text format\nCOPY table_name (col1, col2) FROM stdin WITH (HEADER MATCH);  -- with column list\n```\n\n## 2. Implementation Components\n\n### 2.1 Enum Definition\n**File:** `src/include/commands/copy.h` (lines 26-31)\n\n```c\ntypedef enum CopyHeaderChoice\n{\n\tCOPY_HEADER_FALSE = 0,\n\tCOPY_HEADER_TRUE,\n\tCOPY_HEADER_MATCH,\n} CopyHeaderChoice;\n```\n\nThe enum stores in `CopyFormatOptions.header_line` field.\n\n### 2.2 Grammar Extension\n**File:** `src/backend/parser/gram.y`\n\nThe feature uses the generic COPY option syntax:\n```\nCOPY ... WITH (HEADER value)\n```\n\nWhere `value` can be:\n- Boolean: `true`, `false`, `on`, `off`, `0`, `1`\n- String: `'match'` or `match`\n\nThe grammar accepts this through:\n- `copy_generic_opt_elem` rule (lines 3572-3576)\n- `opt_boolean_or_string` production (lines 1828-1838)\n- Parsed by the generic key-value option handler\n\n### 2.3 Option Processing\n**File:** `src/backend/commands/copy.c`\n\n#### Option Parsing\n- **Lines 603-609:** `ProcessCopyOptions()` calls `defGetCopyHeaderChoice()` for header option\n- **Lines 368-426:** `defGetCopyHeaderChoice()` function handles the parsing:\n  - Accepts strings: \"true\", \"false\", \"on\", \"off\", \"match\" (case-insensitive)\n  - Returns appropriate `CopyHeaderChoice` enum value\n  - **Critical validation (lines 411-415):** Only allows MATCH for COPY FROM, not COPY TO\n  ```c\n  if (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"match\") == 0)\n  {\n      if (!is_from)\n          ereport(ERROR,\n                  (errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n                   errmsg(\"cannot use \\\"%s\\\" with HEADER in COPY TO\", sval)));\n      return COPY_HEADER_MATCH;\n  }\n  ```\n\n#### Binary Mode Validation\n- **Lines 811-815:** Prevents HEADER (including MATCH) in BINARY mode\n  ```c\n  if (opts_out->binary && opts_out->header_line)\n      ereport(ERROR, ...);\n  ```\n\n### 2.4 Header Matching Logic\n**File:** `src/backend/commands/copyfromparse.c` (lines 780-833)\n\n**Function:** `NextCopyFromRawFieldsInternal()`\n\nThe validation happens on the first iteration when `cur_lineno == 0`:\n\n1. **Read header line:** Calls `CopyReadLine()` to read the first line from input\n2. **Parse fields:** Uses either `CopyReadAttributesCSV()` or `CopyReadAttributesText()` to extract field names\n3. **Validate column count:**\n   ```c\n   if (fldct != list_length(cstate->attnumlist))\n       ereport(ERROR, \"wrong number of fields in header line: got %d, expected %d\", ...);\n   ```\n4. **Validate column names:** Iterate through `attnumlist` and compare each field name:\n   ```c\n   foreach(cur, cstate->attnumlist)\n   {\n       // Get the column name from the header\n       colName = cstate->raw_fields[fldnum++];\n       \n       // Get the table's column name\n       Form_pg_attribute attr = TupleDescAttr(tupDesc, attnum - 1);\n       \n       // Compare (case-insensitive using namestrcmp)\n       if (namestrcmp(&attr->attname, colName) != 0)\n           ereport(ERROR, \"column name mismatch...\");\n   }\n   ```\n\n**Key Features:**\n- Works with both CSV and text (tab-delimited) formats\n- Case-insensitive column name comparison using `namestrcmp()`\n- Respects explicitly specified column lists in COPY statement\n- Handles dropped columns correctly (validates against visible columns in `attnumlist`)\n- Provides detailed error messages listing which column mismatched and expected vs. actual names\n\n### 2.5 Regression Tests\n**File:** `src/test/regress/sql/copy.sql` (lines 237-306)\n\nComprehensive test coverage includes:\n\n1. **Success Cases:**\n   - Basic matching headers with all columns\n   - Matching with explicitly specified columns in different order\n   - Matching with both text and CSV formats\n   - Matching after dropped columns\n\n2. **Error Cases:**\n   - Column name mismatch\n   - Missing columns (fewer fields in header than expected)\n   - Extra columns (more fields in header than expected)\n   - Null values in header fields\n   - Dropped columns in header (should fail count mismatch)\n\n3. **Validation Errors:**\n   - Invalid choice: `COPY ... (HEADER wrong_choice)`\n   - COPY TO usage: `COPY ... TO ... (HEADER MATCH)`\n\n**Expected Output:** `src/test/regress/expected/copy.out` (lines 215-278)\n\n## 3.
